<script id="wix-first-paint">
    if (window.ResizeObserver &&
        (!window.PerformanceObserver || !PerformanceObserver.supportedEntryTypes || PerformanceObserver.supportedEntryTypes.indexOf('paint') === -1)) {
        new ResizeObserver(function (entries, observer) {
            entries.some(function (entry) {
                var contentRect = entry.contentRect;
                if (contentRect.width > 0 && contentRect.height > 0) {
                    requestAnimationFrame(function (now) {
                        window.wixFirstPaint = now;
                        dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('wixFirstPaint'));
                    });
                    observer.disconnect();
                    return true;
                }
            });
        }).observe(document.body);
    }
</script>

font-size:34px;" class="font_2 wixui-rich-text__text"><span class="color_15 wixui-rich-text__text">ABOUT US</span></h2>
</div><div id="comp-ifmhp86r" class="comp-ifmhp86r aVng1S wixui-horizontal-line"></div><div id="comp-ifmduswg" class="BaOVQ8 tz5f0K comp-ifmduswg wixui-rich-text" data-testid="richTextElement"><p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="text-align:center; font-size:17px;">Thorne Media is a full service media provider. Award winning producers, writers, directors, editors, animators and coders can guide your project from conception through presentation. We excel at developing project treatments, script writing, field and studio production, post production, VR &amp; AR experiences and app development.</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="text-align:center; font-size:17px;">&nbsp;</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="text-align:center; font-size:17px;">The producers at Thorne Media have over 30 years of experience with all aspects of media production and presentation including Broadcast Television Commercials, Social Media Content, VR &amp; 360 video, Corporate Marketing &amp; Training, Documentaries, Application Development and Live Events.&nbsp;</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="text-align:center; font-size:17px;">&nbsp;</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="text-align:center; font-size:17px;">Thorne Media has continually provided high quality, high impact productions to businesses across the country and indeed, throughout the world. Many high profile companies have chosen us to promote their services, enhance their image, launch&nbsp;products and train their employees. Weve worked on location throughout the United States and internationally throughout Europe, Asia and South America.</p></div></div></div></div><div id="comp-k73oh03n" class="X1aAvp comp-k73oh03n wixui-gallery" role="region" aria-label="Matrix gallery"><div class="zOHRa_ PTgPnj" data-testid="matrix-gallery-items-container"><div class="CRLZg4 shv4DA wixui-gallery__item" data-testid="gallery-item-item" tabindex="-1"><div class="PK3Gze" role="img" data-testid="gallery-item-click-action-disabled" tabindex="0"><div class="cwnvkx"><div class="j_Jt47"><div class="NTOd3P"><wow-image id="img_undefined" class="HlRz5e tuDPQa" data-image-info="{&quot;displayMode&quot;:&quot;fill&quot;,&quot;isLQIP&quot;:true,&quot;imageData&quot;:{&quot;width&quot;:2184,&quot;height&quot;:2184,&quot;uri&quot;:&quot;fee9fb_dd40dff3f1d5407cb4d1b615f8850cd0~mv2_d_2184_2184_s_2.jpg&quot;,&quot;name&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;displayMode&quot;:&quot;fill&quot;}}" data-bg-effect-name="" data-has-ssr-src="" data-src="https://static.wixstatic.com/media/fee9fb_dd40dff3f1d5407cb4d1b615f8850cd0~mv2_d_2184_2184_s_2.jpg/v1/fill/w_291,h_270,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,enc_auto/fee9fb_dd40dff3f1d5407cb4d1b615f8850cd0~mv2_d_2184_2184_s_2.jpg"><img src="https://static.wixstatic.com/media/fee9fb_dd40dff3f1d5407cb4d1b615f8850cd0~mv2_d_2184_2184_s_2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_147,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_auto/fee9fb_dd40dff3f1d5407cb4d1b615f8850cd0~mv2_d_2184_2184_s_2.jpg" alt="" style="width: 233px;
